43006060	Kunsooko ĩĩ, iingĩ muamanigua aakue pĩna alĩ iigilie izi, naaũga, “uLukaani ulu lukakũ! Waani nusũũmile kukulutegeela.”
43006061	ũYesu pĩna numana munkolo yaakue ya kĩna ĩamanigua aakue ĩkĩũlũnga kunsooko ya lukaani ulu, nuaĩĩla, “Lwalu lwamukũmpiane?
43006062	Ikitũla mbii gua kanga mumuone uMuana-muntu winankĩla kĩna alĩ wĩĩlĩĩ umuandio?
43006063	ĩNkolo, ĩĩo yukupangatagiaa, umuĩlĩ sika ũjĩpĩĩle kakĩntu, iNkaani nalĩ nukumuĩĩla ingĩ nkolo, kangĩ upanga.
43006064	Ĩpa akoolĩ mumiani nasika asuĩlĩĩle.” Kuitĩ ũYesu alumanile kwipũna umuandio aani nasika asuĩlĩĩle, kangĩ waani nukakumusakia.
43006065	Nuũga, “Kunsooko ĩĩ aza mumuĩĩlĩĩle kĩna ukutilĩ nusũũmile kwiiiza kumuane kanga ĩsika mupeegue nuTata.”
43006066	Kwipũna paapo iingĩ muamanigua aakue naashooka kĩnũũma, sika naĩtiata nduyo.
43006067	Paapo ũYesu nuaĩĩla naikyumi naabĩlĩ, “Niniinie gaa mwasiiane kwilega?”
43006068	uSimoni Petelo numushookeelia, “Shekulu, kwende kwa kuani? Ue utĩĩte inkaani za upanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ,
43006069	nindiishie kwasuĩlĩĩle nukwilĩnga kĩna ue ingĩ uMuelu wa kĩNzua.”
43006070	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Sika alĩ numusaaguĩlene inie namwikyumi naabĩlĩ. Nuumuĩ waani ingĩ shetani?”
43006071	Alumugambile ũYuda ũsha Simoni nwa kuIsakaliote; uuyo numuĩ mwikyumi naabĩlĩ, nũjile kumusakia.
43007001	Pembele ũYesu nũipilima muGalĩlaya; sika nusiia kwipilima muUyahũdi kunsooko ĩAyahũdi alĩ idũũma kukumuulaga.
43007002	Nulutondo nalukulu lwa Ayahũdi lwa pigũnda alĩ lwĩpiipĩ.
43007003	Luulo gua, ĩanũna aakue naamuĩĩla, “Lega ĩpa, wende kuUyahũdi koona ĩamanigua aako aone ĩmĩlĩmo yaako nukuĩtuma.
43007004	Kuitĩ kutilĩ kamuntu nukutenda ulukaani kukĩmpisĩ-mpisĩ, nduyo umuene usiile kukigyelela. Kanga utende itĩ, igyelelie kuunkũmbigyulu.”
43007005	Kuitĩ sunga ĩanũna aakue sika alĩ asuĩlĩĩle mumuakue.
43007006	Luulo ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “ityũngo liane likaalĩ kalapika, ĩpa ityũngo liani lĩkoolĩ intondo tũlũ.
43007007	uUnkũmbigyulu sika wishũũma kukumusuukĩlua inie; ukunsuukĩlaguaa uneene kunsooko ĩne nukuukuĩlaa kĩna uutendi waakue ingĩ ubĩĩ.
43007008	Nankĩlĩ uniinie muende kulutondo nalukulu; ĩne nikĩĩlĩ kalanankĩla kwienda kulutondo nalukulu luasio, kuitĩ ityũngo likaalĩ kalakonda.”
43007009	Pĩna nuaĩĩla izi, nwikyala muGalĩlaya.
43007010	Pĩna ĩanũna aakue naanankĩla kwienda kulutondo nalukulu, paapo nduzo nunankĩla, sika kukualiĩ, alĩ zĩ kukĩmpisĩ-mpisĩ.
43007011	Iio gua ĩAyahũdi naaa kumudũũma mulutondo nalukulu, naaũga, “Wĩĩlĩ mpĩĩ unuasio?”
43007012	Na wĩĩ wĩng'ũng'ũntia wingĩ mumulundo kunsooko yaakue ĩĩĩa naaũga, “Muntu muuza,” ĩĩĩa naaũga, “Zũi, ĩpa ukualimĩĩlia ĩantu.”
43007013	Ĩpa kutilĩ naalumutambuĩle paantu kunsooko ya koopoka ĩAyahũdi.
43007014	Muntondo za lutondo nalukulu ũYesu nunankĩla nũingĩlla muNumba yakĩNzua nũimania.
43007015	ĩAyahũdi nakulĩlua, naaũga, “Uyu umanile mbii ĩmĩlimu pĩna sika mulangue?”
43007016	ũYesu nuashookeelia nuũga, “uUmania waane sika waane, ingĩ waakue naaluntumile.
43007017	Wensi kanga waloogue kwitenda uulooa waakue, ukakuulĩnga uumanigua uu, kĩna upũnile kwa kĩNzua katia nĩkĩtambulĩlia ning'ene.
43007018	Uyu nukĩtambulĩlagiaa wing'ene ukudũũmaa ulukũmo luakue umuene; ĩpa uzo nukudũumaa ulukũmo luakue naalumutumile, uuyo wa tai-taaii nuwoononi ukutilĩ mumuakue.
43007019	Naalumupĩĩle inie uUlagĩĩlio sika Musane? Sunga ukutilĩ kumiani nukuukendegelaa uUlagĩĩlio. Nĩkĩ mwinduuma kwimbulaga.”
43007020	iYũmbĩ nalĩshookeelia, “Ue umunalĩsĩĩmuĩ! Waani nwidũũma kukukuulaga?”
43007021	ũYesu nushookeelia nuaĩĩla, “Alĩ ntendile utendi umuĩ, tũlũ ensi namukulĩlua.
43007022	Kunsooko ĩĩ uMusa numupeela uwaalami; (sika upũnile kwa kĩ Musa, ĩpa alĩ kuatata aani), niniinie mulutondo lwa wikyali mukualamagiaa umuntu.
43007023	Muntu kanga waalamigue palutondo lwa wikyali, uUlagĩĩlio wa kĩMusa ulekioononua, nĩkĩ mwintakĩla kunsooko namukamagiaa umuntu palutondo lwa wikyali?
43007024	Mulekilamula kunzi udũũ, taazu mulamule ĩkulukuuluu.”
43007025	Luulo gua, ĩaniYelusalemũ ĩamuĩ naaũga, “Sika wayune naakumudũũmaa amuulage?
43007026	Laaĩ gua, witambula kualiĩ, sika akumuĩĩla kalukaani! ĩAkulu ĩĩtu alĩngile ĩtaine kĩna uyu ingĩ Kilisito?
43007027	Ĩpa uyu kumumanile kĩna upũnile. Iio uKilisito pĩna ukiiiza, ukutilĩ numanile kĩna upũnile.”
43007028	Luulo ũYesu nwĩtunta ululi muNumba ya kĩNzua, nũmania nuũga, “Ĩne munzĩzĩ, nĩkĩna mpũnile muĩzĩ; sunga sika nĩĩzĩĩle uneene, ĩpa naaluntumile ingĩ wa tai, niniinie sika mumuĩzĩ.
43007029	Ĩne numuĩzĩ kunsooko mpũnile kumuakue, nduyo muene untumile.”
43007030	Luulo gua naandũũma kukumuguĩla, ĩpa kutilĩ naalumutualĩlĩĩle umukono, kunsooko ityũngo liakue sika alĩ lyalaaza.
43007031	Iingĩ mwiyũmbĩ naasuĩĩla mumuakue, naaũga, “Pĩna wijiliiiza uKilisito, ũjilitenda ilĩngasĩĩllio iingĩne kwikĩla naalutendile uyu?”
43007032	ĩApalisayo naaligyũlia iyũmbĩ lĩkĩũlũnga izi kunsooko yaakue; paapo ĩapolia naakulu nĩApalisayo naatuma ĩĩtumi amuguĩle.
43007033	ũYesu nuũga, “Tyũngo niino kĩlĩ nĩpalumuĩ niniinie; nonguĩle kumuakue naaluntumile.
43007034	Mukindũũma, sika mukimona, nineene pĩna nĩĩlĩ inie sika mwishũũma kwiiiza.”
43007035	Paapo ĩAyahũdi naĩtambuĩla eene kuene, “Ulomile wende mpĩĩ uyu itĩ kuleke kumuona ishie. Ukienda kuupalansano wa Agilikine nukukuamania ĩAgiliki?
43007036	Lukaani kĩ ulu naazulutambuĩle, Mukindũũma, sika mukimona; nineene pĩna nĩĩlĩ inie sika mwishũũma kwiiiza?”
43007037	Palutondo nalukulu nangũlũ, lwa mumalĩĩlio lwa ntondo nankulu, ũYeu nuĩmĩka nwĩtuntĩkia nuũga, “Tũlũ wensi kanga wakolue ĩnoota waaze kumuane wakope.
43007038	Nusuĩlĩĩle mumuane kĩna uwandĩkua uũgile, miongo ya maazĩ ma upanga ikipũna munsĩ yaakue.”
43007039	Alutambuĩle itĩ mumpola za kĩMuau naĩkakumuanũnkula naasuĩlĩĩle mumuakue, kuitĩ uMuau alĩ wikĩĩlĩ kalakigyelela, kunsooko ũYesu alĩ wikĩĩlĩĩ wakuligue
43007040	Paapo ĩĩĩa kwipuna mwiyũmbĩ pĩna naaziigia inkaani izi naaũga, “Tai uyu wayu munakĩdagu nuasio.”
43007041	Naĩngĩ naaũga, Uyu wayu Kilisito. ĩĨĩa naaũga, “Mbii gua, uKilisito wapũna kũGalilayan?
43007042	uWandĩkua sika alĩ uũgilene kĩna uKilisito upũnile muluuli lwa kĩDaudi, muBetelehemũ ĩkĩsaalĩ naalĩ wĩĩlĩ uDaudi?”
43007043	Paapo nautũla ukamatuki mwiyũmbĩ kunsooko yaakue.
43007044	ĩAmuĩ aao nasiia amuguĩle, ĩpa kutilĩ naalumutualĩlĩĩle ĩmĩkono.
43007045	Paapo ĩĩtumi naaaza kuapolia naakulu nĩApalisayo ndĩo naaaĩĩla, “Nĩkĩ sika mwamuleeta?”
43007046	ĩĨtumi naashookeelia, “Kutilĩ kamuntu nukutambulaa kĩna umuntu nuasio nwitambula!”
43007047	Paapo ĩApalisayo naashookeelia, “Niniinie mwapuutagiguaane?
43007048	Waani gua muakulu katia muApalisayo naasuĩlĩĩle mumuakue?
43007049	Ĩpa iyũmbĩ ĩlĩ nasika lĩlĩngile uulagĩĩlio lyazũmaguaa.”
43007050	uNikodemo, uyo naalumuuzĩlĩĩle mbele, naalĩ umuĩ waao, nuaĩĩla,
43007051	“Mbii, uUlagĩĩlio wĩĩtu ukulamulaane umuntu pĩna sika waliigiguaa tangua nukwimana kĩna utendile yaani?”
43007052	Nashookeelia naamuĩĩla, “Nunduue upũnile kũGalilayane? Dũũma, uoone kĩna kutilĩ kamunakĩdagu naalũgyelĩĩle kwipũna kũGalilaya.”
43008001	ĩpa ũYesu nulongola kunkonko ya mĩzeituni.
43008002	ĩKĩĩlĩma pĩna nakiungua nũingĩla kangĩ muNumba ya kĩNzua. ĩAntu ensi naamuagaana; nwikyalansa nuĩ kuamania.
43008003	ĩAlangi nĩApalisayo naamuleetela musungu naalĩ mukũngue muugalolia; naamuĩmĩkia pakatĩ,
43008004	Naamuĩĩla, “Mumania, umusungu uzu aza mukũngue pĩna aza wigololia
43008005	muUlagĩĩlio uMusa alukulagĩlĩĩlie ĩaasiio atũlue magũe; ĩpa ue uũgĩleeii?”
43008006	Naatambula itĩ kukumugema, koona aligie nsooko ya kumusokia. ũYesu nutũna pansĩ, nuandĩka mumasalu naluala.
43008007	Pĩna naĩkakia kukumukolia, nuĩmĩka nuaĩĩla, “Namugila kautimu mumiani nuĩ wa muandio kukumusũtia igyũe.”
43008008	Nutũna pansĩ kangĩ, nuandĩka mumasalu
43008009	Ndĩo pĩna naiigia, naasokigua nĩmiioo yaao, naapũna umuĩ umuĩ, naandia ĩanampala sunga nwa mumalĩĩlio. Nusaaga ũYesu wing'ene numusungu wĩĩmĩkile pakatĩ
43008010	ũYesu nuuuka, sika numuona kaumuĩ ĩpa umusungu udũũ. Numuĩĩla, “Musungu ue, ĩĩlĩ mpĩĩ aasio ĩasokia aako? Ukutilĩne nwa kukulamula kĩna umutimu?”
43008011	Numuĩĩla, “Kutilĩ Shekulu.” ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Nineene gaa sika nukukulamula. Longola ulekitimula kangĩ.”]
43008012	Paapo kangĩ ũYesu nuaĩĩla nuũga, “Ĩne neene nĩweelu wa unkũmbigyulu; nwa kuntiata ĩne sika ukigendela mukiiti, ĩpa ukaa utĩĩte uweelu wa upanga.”
43008013	Iio gua ĩApalisayo naamuĩĩla, “Ue wĩkuĩlĩĩle wing'ene; uukuĩli waako sika wa tai.”
43008014	ũYesu nushookeelia nuaĩĩla, “Kanga ĩne ĩnĩkuĩlĩĩle ning'ene nakĩ, uukuĩli waane ingĩ wa tai, kuitĩ nĩĩzĩ kĩna mpũnile nĩkĩna nunziĩ. Inie gua sika mumanile kĩna mpũnile nĩkĩna nunziĩ.
43008015	Inie mwilamula kukĩmuĩlĩĩ ĩne gua sika nukumulamulaa kaumuĩ.
43008016	Kanga ĩne ĩnilamula nakĩ, uulamuli waane ingĩ wa tai, kuitĩ ĩne sika ning'ene nanukulamulaa, ĩpa uneene ninduyo naaluntumile.
43008017	Sunga muUlagĩĩliio waani yandĩkue kĩna uukuĩli wa antu abĩlĩ ingĩ wa tai.
43008018	Ĩne neene nanĩkuĩlĩĩle uneene, nuTata naaluntumile unkuĩlĩĩle.”
43008019	Paapo naamuĩĩla, Ushoo wĩĩlĩĩ mpĩĩ? ũYesu nushookeelia, “Sika mumanile ĩne sunga uTata sika mumumaile. Kanga ĩmumanile ĩne, alĩ mũjile kumumana nuTata waane.”
43008020	iNkaani izi alutambuĩle nũmania muNumba ya kĩNzua, nwĩpaapo pauĩĩkĩlo wa sadaka. Kutilĩ naalumuguĩlile, kuitĩ ityũngo liakue sika alĩ lyalaaza.
43008021	Paapo ũYesu nuaĩĩla kangĩ, “Ĩne nalega, niniinie mukindũũma; mukikia mumulandu waani; kĩna nunziĩ ĩne, inie sika musũũmile kwiiiza.”
43008022	Paapo ĩAyahũdi naaũga, “Mbii gua, ukakĩulagane; kuitĩ nwiũga, kĩna nunziĩ sika mwishũũma kwiiiza?”
43008023	Nuaĩĩla, “Inie mwa pĩna pansĩ; ĩne na kukiania; iinie mwa unkũmbigyulu uu; ĩne sika na muna unkũmbigyulu uu.
43008024	Aza namuĩĩla mukikia mumĩlandu yani kuitĩ kanga musiitishuĩĩla kĩna ingĩ neene, mukikia mumĩlandu yaani.”
43008025	Paapo naamuĩĩla, “Ue uue waani?” ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Lwalu naaza namuĩĩla kwipũna umuanidio.
43008026	Ntĩĩte ningĩ za kutambula nukwilamula kumuani; ĩpa uzo naaluntumile ingĩ wa tai, nineene naalĩ nĩziigilie kumuakue, ziizo nukutambulaa muna unkũmbigyulu.”
43008027	Sika naalĩnga kĩna ukuaĩĩla za kĩTata.
43008028	Paapo ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Pĩna mukakumunansula uMuana-muntu, paapo mukilĩnga kĩna ingĩ neene, kangĩ kutilĩ nanukulutenda ning'ene, ĩpa kĩna uTata naalumanilie ĩne, ziizo nukuzitambula.
43008029	Nduyo naaluntumile wayu kwĩpalumuĩ nineene, sikundekile ning'ene, kuitĩ ĩne nukutendaa intondo tũlũ nazumuloelĩĩlie uyo.”
43008030	Pĩna alĩ witambula izi, iingĩ naasuĩĩla mumuakue.
43008031	ũYesu nuaĩĩla ĩAyahũdi naalĩ amusuĩlĩĩle, “Inie kanga mwikyale mulukaani luane, ĩtai mwĩamanigua aane;
43008032	Mukakumĩlĩnga ĩtai, nĩtai ĩkakumutenda akolelua.”
43008033	Naamushookeelia, “Ishie kwĩluuli lwa kĩIbũlahimu; sika kwalatũla asese kumuntu wensi intondo tũlũ. Wiũgaaii, mukitendua akolelua?”
43008034	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, Tũlũ wensi nukutendaa umulandu ingĩ musese wa mulandu.
43008035	uMusese sika ukikyalaa munumba ĩkalĩ nakalĩ; umuana ukikyalaa ĩkalĩ nakalĩ.
43008036	Iio gua uMuana kanga wamutende akolelua, ĩtaĩ mukitũla akolelua.
43008037	Maniile kĩna mualĩĩ luuli lwa kĩIbũlahimu, ĩpa mwidũũma kumbulaga kunsooko ulukaani luane lugila kalioma munsĩ yaani.
43008038	Naalĩ nizioonie kwa kĩTata, ziizo nukuzitambulaa. Niniinie namuziigilie kwa kĩTata waani, ziizo mukuzitendaa.”
43008039	Naashookeelia naamuĩĩla, “uTata wĩĩtu ingĩ uIbũlahimu.” ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Kanga ĩmwĩaana a kĩIbũlahimu aza mũjile kuĩtenda ĩmĩlĩmo ya kĩIbũlahimu.
43008040	Ĩpaino mwidũũma kwimbulaga ĩne, nanumuntu nanukumuĩĩlaa ĩtai naalĩ nĩmiigilie kwa kĩNzua. uIbũlahimu sika alutendile itĩ.”
43008041	Inie mukĩtuma ĩmĩlĩmo ya kĩTata waani. Naamuĩĩla, “Ishie sika kualelue mumĩgololio; kutĩĩte uTata umuĩ, uNzua.”
43008042	ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Kanga uNzua ĩTata waani aza mujilindoogua nineene, kuitĩ nijile mpũnile kwa kĩNzua; sika nijile ning'ene, ĩpa muene aluntumile.
43008043	Nĩkĩ mwasiitilĩnga uutambuli waane? Ingĩ kunsooko sika mwishũũma kwiiigia ulukani luane.
43008044	Inie mwa kĩtata waani Shetani, ninshula za kĩtata waani mualoe kukuzitenda. uNuasio alĩ muulagani kwipũna iyuukĩ, sunga sika ukuĩmaa mutai, kuitĩ ĩtai yukutilĩ mumuakue. Pĩna witambula ulongo ukutaambulaa ĩzaakue muene, kunsooko ingĩ mulongo, kangĩ tata wa ulongo.
43008045	Nineene, kunsooko nukumĩtambula ĩtai, sika mwishuĩĩla.
43008046	Waani kumiami nukuĩlĩĩle kĩna numunamĩlandu? Kanga ĩnitambula ĩtai, nĩkĩ sika mwinshuĩĩla?
43008047	Nwa kĩNzua ukuziigagiaa inkaani za kĩNzua. Luulo inie sika mukũigagiaa kunsooko inie sika mwa kĩNzua.”
43008048	ĩAyahũdi naashookeelia naamuĩĩla, “Sika kwitambula iizane kĩna ue uMusamalia, kangĩ umunalĩsĩĩmuĩ?”
43008049	ũYesu nushookeelia, “Ĩne sika numunalĩsĩĩmuĩ, ĩpa nukumukulia uTata waane. Niniinie mukumelaa ĩne.
43008050	Ĩne sika nidũũma uukulu waane, ukoolĩ nwĩdũũma nukwilamula.
43008051	Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, tũlũ wensi kanga wakendegeele ulukaani luane sika ukiona kaukiu sunga ĩkalĩ nakalĩ.”
43008052	ĩAyahũdi naamuĩĩla, “Ĩpa kwalĩnga kĩna umunalĩsĩĩmuĩ ue. uIbũlahimu nukia nĩanakĩdagu, ninduue wiũga, Tũlũ wensi kanga wakendegeele ulukaani luane sika ukilũla kaukiu sunga ĩkalĩ nakalĩ.
43008053	Ue umukulune kwikĩla utata wĩĩtu uIbũlahimu, nduyo wakiile, nĩanakĩdagu naakia! ukĩtenda wĩwaani?”
43008054	ũYesu nushookeelia, “Kanga nĩkulie uneene, uukulu waane sika kĩntu. Nukunkulagiaa ingĩ uTata waane namukumutambulaa inie kĩna ingĩ Nzua waani.
43008055	Niniinie sika mumumanile, ĩpa ĩne numumanile. Kangambũge sika numumanile nikitũla mulongo zĩ uniinie; ĩpa numumanile, nulukaani luakue nulukendegelĩĩle.
43008056	uIbũlahimu utata waani alĩ muloekigue waone ulutondo luane; nuluona, nulumba.”
43008057	Luulo gua ĩAyahũdi naamuĩĩla, “Sika walagela ĩmiaka makumi mataano; wamuonilene uIbũlahimu?”
43008058	ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, pĩna uIbũlahimu alĩ wikaalĩ, ĩne nankoolĩ.”
43008059	Paapo naasola ĩmagũe amusũtie. ũYesu nwĩpisa nulega muNumba ya kĩNzua.
43009001	Pĩna nulongola numuona muntu mupokũ kwipũna kuulelua waakue.
43009002	ĩAmanigua aakue naamukolia naaũga, “Shekulu, waani alutimuĩle, uyune kanga aleli aakue, walelue mupokũ?”
43009003	ũYesu nushookeelia, “Uyu sika utimuĩle sunga ĩaleli aakue, ĩpa umulĩmo wa kĩNzua wigyeleligue kumuakue.
43009004	Yukũjĩpĩĩle ishie kukĩtuma ĩmĩlĩmo yaakue naaluntumile pĩna kĩlĩ munsĩ. Utiku ukiiiza ukilemua kaumuĩ kukĩtuma umulĩmo.
43009005	Pĩna kĩlĩ nkoolĩ muna unkũmbigyulu, ĩne neene weelu wa unkũmbigyulu.”
43009006	Pĩna nutambula izi, nutia ĩmatĩ pansĩ, nulũa ilyolo, numupaka umupokũ mumiiso maakue kumalolo maasio.
43009007	Numuĩĩla, “Longola, ukalale mwilyambo lya Siloamu” (ndogolelio yaakue Namutumue). Paapo nulongola nukalala, nushooka waaziiona.
43009008	Iio gua ĩanakaa aakue nĩaasio naalĩ amuoonie ĩmbele kĩna alĩ mulompi naaũga, “Sika wayune alukuuzaa wikyalansile nukwilompana?”
43009009	ĩĨĩa naaũga, “Wayuuyu.” Naĩngĩ naaũga, “Zũi, ĩpa wĩpianile ninduyo.” Uzo nuũga, “Ingĩ neene.”
43009010	Paapo naamukolia, “ĩmiiso maako malaĩliguaa mbii?”
43009011	uNuasio nushookeelia, “Muntu nukuĩtaguaa Yesu nulũa ilyolo, numpaka ĩmiiso maane, numbuĩla, ‘Longola kuSiloamu ukalale.’ Paapo nanongola nankalala, namona.”
43009012	Naamuĩĩla, “uNuasio wĩĩlĩĩ mpĩĩ?” Nuũga, “Magu.”
43009013	Naalĩ mupokũ naamutuala kuApalisayo.
43009014	Alĩ lutondo lwa wikyali pĩna ũYesu alulũile ilyolo nukukumulaĩlia ĩmiiso.
43009015	ĩApalisayo namukolia kangĩ, “Alumulaĩligue mbii. Nuaĩĩla, Numpaka malolo ĩmiiso maane, nankalala, namona.”
43009016	Iio gua, ĩApalisayo ĩamuĩ naaũga, “uMuntu uyu sikupũnile kwa kĩNzua kunsooko sikukulukendegeela ulutondo lwa wikyali.” Naĩngĩ naaũga, “Wishũũma mbii umunamĩlandu kwitenda iilĩngasĩĩlio kĩna ii?” Nautũla ukamatuki mumiao.
43009017	Iio naamuĩĩla umupokũ kangĩ, “Ue wiũgaaii mumpola zaakue, kuitĩ wakulaĩlagiaa ĩmiiso?” Nuũga, “Ingĩ munakĩdagu.”
43009018	ĩAyahũdi sika naasuĩĩla impola zaakue kĩna alĩ mupokũ nukwilaĩligua, sunga naaĩĩta ĩaleli aakue naalĩ mulaĩligue.
43009019	Naakolia naaũga, “Uyu wayu muana wanine namukuũgaa kĩna alĩ mulelue mupokũ. ĩpaino waiona mbii?”
43009020	ĩAleli aakue naashookeelia naaũga, “Kumanile kĩna uyu muana wĩĩtu nduyo alĩ mupokũ;
43009021	ĩpa sika kumanile kĩna waaziiona mbii ĩpanio, kanga waani magu numulaĩĩlie ĩmiiso sika kumanile, mukoliĩ, uyo muntu mukulu, wĩtambulĩlie umuene.”
43009022	ĩAleli aakue alĩ itambula izi kunsooko alĩ aoopookile ĩAyahũdi, kuitĩ ĩAyahũdi alĩ akondilie kwikomia ĩkialo tũlũ wensi kanga wamukuĩle uKilisito, wakamatulue mũshũnagogi.
43009023	Luulo gua ĩaleli aakue naaũga, “Uzo muntu mukulu, mukoliĩ umuene.”
43009024	Paapo naamuĩta kaubĩlĩ umuntu naalĩ mupokũ, naamuĩĩla, “Umukũmuukie uNzua, ishe kumanile kĩna umuntu uyu munamĩlanndu.”
43009025	uNuasio nushookeelia, “Kanga ĩmunamĩlandu magu sika manile; manile luuluu lumuĩ, alĩ numupokũ ĩpaino naaziona.”
43009026	Naamuĩĩla, “Azukutendile yaani? Azukulaĩĩlie mbii ĩmiiso?”
43009027	Nuashookeelia, “Nakondagiaa kukumuĩĩla, sika mũigilie? Nĩkĩ mualoe kwiiigia kangĩ? Niniinie mwaloaguaane kwitũla amanigua aakue?”
43009028	Naamutuka, naaũga, “Ue umumanigua waakue unuasio; ishie kuamanigua a kĩMusa.
43009029	Ishie kumanile kĩna uNzua alutambuĩle kwa kĩMusa; ĩpa uyu sika kumanile kĩna upũnile.”
43009030	Umuntu nuasio nushookeelia nuaĩĩla, “uLukaani ulu lwa ukulĩlua! Kĩna inie sika mumanile kĩna upũnile, nduyo nundaĩlia ĩmiiso.
43009031	Kumanile kĩna uNzua sika ukuiigagiaa ĩanamĩlandu, ĩpa wensi kanga wamukulie uNzua nukwitenda uulooa waakue, unuasio uuyo ukumũigagiaa.
43009032	Kwipũna iyuukĩ sika yaliigigua kĩna muntu wensi ulaĩĩlie ĩmiiso ma muntu naalĩ mulelue mupokũ.
43009033	Kanga uyu ĩsika alupũnile kwa kĩNzua sika azũjilishũũma kwitenda kalukaani.”
43009034	Naashookeelia naamuĩĩla, “Ue alumulelue mumĩlandu mĩtilĩ, ninduuene wakukumania ishie?” Naamuguma kunzi.
43009035	ũYesu nuigia kĩna alĩ amugumile kunzi, numuona nuũga, “Ue usuĩlĩĩlene mwa kĩMuana-muntu?”
43009036	uNuasio nushookeelia nuũga, “Waani Shekulu, koona nsuĩĩle mumuakue.”
43009037	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Wamuonaa. Wazu nwitambula ninduue ingĩ muene.”
43009038	Nuũga, “Nasuĩĩla Shekulu.” Numutũngamĩla.
43009039	ũYesu nuũga, “Ĩne nijile muna unkũmbigyulu uu kuulamuli, itĩ nasika akuonaa aone, ndĩo nakuonaa atũle apokũ.”
43009040	ĩApalisayo naalĩ yĩensi ninduyo naiigia izi, naamuĩĩla, “Kuapokũne sunga nindiishie?”
43009041	ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Kanga ĩmuapokũ, sika aza mwijilitũla nĩmĩlandu; ĩpa muũgile, Kukuonaa; ĩmĩlandu yaani ĩkoolĩ.”
43010001	“Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, nasika ukũingĩĩlaa pamulango wa mpongolo wa nkolo ĩpa wapũũtĩle pĩngĩ, unuasio ingĩ mũii kangĩ muleegelania.
43010002	Nukũingĩlĩlaa pamulango ingĩ umudĩĩmi wa nkolo.
43010003	uMulindĩĩla-mulango ukumũgyuĩlaa uyo, ninkolo zukumũigagiaa ululi luakue; ukuita inkolo zaakue kumiina maao nukukuzintongeela kunzi.
43010004	Pĩna wazipũnia tũlũ ĩzaakue ukuzitongeelaa, ninkolo zukumutiataa kunsooko zimanile ululi luakue.
43010005	uMugenda sika zukumutiataa, ĩpa zukumutalamaa kunsooko sika zulumanile ululi lwa mugenda.”
43010006	ũYesu nuaĩĩla ĩmpiani ĩĩ, ĩpa ĩaasio sika naalĩnga naalukuaĩĩla.
43010007	Iio ũYesu nuũga kangĩ, “Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, Ĩne neene numulango wa nkolo.
43010008	Tũlũ ensi naalĩ antongelĩĩle ingĩ iii nĩaleegelania ĩpa inkolo sika nazĩiigia.
43010009	Ine neene numulango; tũlũ wensi kanga wingĩlĩle pamuane ukigũnĩka; ukiingĩla nukwipũna, ukiligia udĩĩmo.
43010010	uMũii sika ukuuzaa isiitituũla wiie, waulage nukwioonona; ĩne nijile zitũle nuupanga, kangĩ zĩĩ nduo wingĩ dũũ.
43010011	“Ĩne neene numudĩĩmi namuuza. uMudĩĩmi namuuza ukuupũnagiaa uumĩ waakue kunsooko ya nkolo.
43010012	uMutiĩkia nasika mudĩĩmi ninkolo ĩsika zaakue, ukumuonaa ũyĩngi upolokile, ukuzilekaa inkolo, ukumankaa; nũyĩngi ukuziguĩlaa nukukuzishapatĩlia,
43010013	Kunsooko uyo mutiĩkia, sika ukukunkunalaa kunsooko ya nkolo.
43010014	Ĩne neene numudĩĩmi namuuza; ĩzaane nĩzimanile nĩzaane zimanile ĩne,
43010015	kĩna uTata numanile ĩne nineene numumanile uTata; nuuumĩ waane nuupũnilie kunsooko ya nkolo.
43010016	Ninkolo nzia nĩzitĩĩte nasika za mumpongolo ĩĩ; nindizo injĩpĩĩle nĩzileete, nululi luane zĩkakulũigia, nalĩkitũla dyale lĩmuĩ numudĩĩmi umuĩ.
43010017	“Luulo gua uTata undoilue kunsooko nuupũnilie uuumi waane, koona nuusole kangĩ.
43010018	Ukutilĩ nukundeegelagiaa, ĩpa ĩne nuupũnilie uneene. Ntĩĩte usũũmi wa kuupũnua; ntĩĩte usũũmi wa kuusola kangĩ. Ilyangĩĩlio ĩlĩ alĩ naanũnkuĩle kwa kĩTata waane.”
43010019	Nautũla ukamatuki muAyahũdi kunsooko ya nkaani izi.
43010020	ĩĨĩa naaũga, “munalĩsĩĩmuĩ, kangĩ wasalile, nĩkĩ mukumutegeela.”
43010021	ĩĨĩa naaũga “iNkaani izi sika za munalĩsĩĩmuĩ. ĩLĩsĩĩmuĩ lishũũmane kwilaĩlia ĩmiiso maapokũ.”
43010022	Naluĩ lutondo nalukulu lwaa kumielia ĩNumba ya kĩNzua mũYelusalemũ, intondo za nĩmĩla pĩna yukuguaa.
43010023	ũYesu nũiumba-umba muNumba ya kĩNzua mukĩanda kya kĩSolomoni.
43010024	Paapo ĩAyahũdi naamupilimĩkĩĩlia, naamuĩĩla, “Sunga nzuakĩ ukikungualia inkolo zĩĩtu? Kanga ue ĩwĩKilisito kuĩĩle kualiĩ.”
43010025	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Alĩ namuĩĩlĩĩle, niniinie sika mwishuĩĩla. ĩMĩlĩmo nanĩkĩtumaa kuliina lya kĩTata waane, ĩĩo ĩnkuĩlĩĩle ĩne.
43010026	Ĩpa inie sika musuĩlĩĩle kunsooko inie sika mukoolĩ munkolo zaane.
43010027	iNkolo zaane zukũigagiaa ululi luane nineene nĩzimanile, ndizo zukuntiataa.
43010028	Nineene nukuzipeelaa upanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ, sika zikilimĩĩla ĩkalĩ nakalĩ; ukutilĩ nukakuzikamantuula mumukono waane.
43010029	uTata waane numpĩĩle ĩzaasio ingĩ mukulu kwikĩla tũlũ; ukutilĩ nusũũmile kukuzikamantuula mumukoono wa kĩTata.
43010030	Ĩne nuTata kwĩumuĩ.”
43010031	ĩAyahũdi naasoleela ĩmagũe kangĩ koona amutũle.
43010032	ũYesu nushookeelia, “Numulagĩlĩĩle mĩlĩmo mingĩ namĩĩza nĩpũnile kwa kĩTata. Mumĩlĩmo ĩĩ, nuĩmbĩ namwintũlĩla ĩmagũe?”
43010033	ĩAyahũdi naamushookeelia, “Kunsooko ya utendi nauuza sika kukukutũla ĩmagũe, ĩpa kunsooko ya utukĩli, kuitĩ ue nwĩmuntu ukĩtenda wĩNzua.”
43010034	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Sika yandĩkuene muUlagĩĩlio waani, ĩne mbũgile, Inie muanzua?
43010035	Kanga alĩĩ uĩĩtile anzua ĩaasio naalĩ aagaanue nulukaani lwa kĩNzua (nuwandĩkua sika usũũmile kwioononua),
43010036	ĩne uTata naalunzelilie, nuntuma muna unkũmbigyulu, inie mwiũgaaii kĩna natuka, kunsooko aza mbũgile, Ĩne nĩMuanawa kĩNzua?
43010037	Kanga ĩsika nukuĩtendaa ĩmĩlĩmo ya kĩTata waane, mulekinshuĩĩla.
43010038	Kanga ĩnukuĩtendaa, anga musitinshuĩĩla ĩne noo, muĩsuĩĩle ĩmĩlĩmo, koona mumane nukwilĩnga kĩna uTata umoolĩ mumuane nineene moolĩ mwa kĩTata.”
43010039	Paapo naadũũma kukumuguĩla kangĩ; nulega mumĩkono yaao.
43010040	Nuenda kangĩ kwityumbĩ liYolidani, paapo pĩna uYohana alukoolĩ ĩmbele nũbadĩĩzia; nwikyala kuuko.
43010041	Iingĩ naamuagaana, naaũga, “uYohana sikaalutendile kĩlĩngasĩĩlio kakĩmuĩ, ĩpa zensi naalutambuĩle uYohana mumpola za kĩuyu alĩ za tai.”
43010042	Iingĩ naasuĩĩla mumuakue kuasio.
43011001	Alukoolĩ muluĩle, umuĩ, uLazalo wa kuBetania, kukĩsaalĩ kya kĩMalia nuMalita umunũna waakue.
43011002	Alĩ uMalia uuyo naalumupakile ũShekulu ĩmaakũta nukukumupiagula ĩmĩgulu yaakue kumatũmbĩ maakue; numugũlĩ waakue uLazalo alĩ muluĩle.
43011003	Iio gua, ĩagũlĩ naamutualĩla impola, naaũga, “Shekulu laaa, numuloilue waazaa muluĩle.”
43011004	ũYesu pĩna nũigia, nuũga, “uUluĩle uu sika wa nkia, ĩpa kunsooko ya ukulu wa kĩNzua, koona uMuana wa kĩNzua wakuligue kuwaasio.”
43011005	ũYesu alualoilue uMalita numunũna waakue nuLazalo.
43011006	Luulo, pĩna nũigia kĩna waazaa muluĩle, nwikyala ntondo zibĩlĩ paapo pĩna alĩ wĩĩlĩ.
43011007	Pembele nuaĩĩla ĩamanigua aakue, “Kuĩni kuUyahũdi kangĩ.”
43011008	ĩAmanigua naamuĩĩla, “Shekulu, ijuli-juulii ĩAyahũdi alĩ idũũma akutũle ĩmagũe; ukiendane kangĩ kuasio?”
43011009	ũYesu nushookeelia, “iNsaa za munsĩ sika kyumi nazibĩlĩne? Tũlũ wensi kanga wagende ĩmunsĩ sika ukukũmpaa kunsooko ukuuonaa uweelu wa unkũmbigyulu uu.
43011010	Tũlũ wensi kanga wagende uutiku ukukũmpaa kunsooko uweelu ukutilĩ mumuakue.”
43011011	Nutaambula izi, pembele nuaĩĩla, “uLazalo umusuamĩĩĩtu wagonile ndoolo, ĩpa nalongola kukumulaĩlia.”
43011012	Paapo ĩamanigua aakue naamuĩĩla, “Shekulu, kanga ĩugonile ndoolo ukikamia.”
43011013	Ĩpa ũYesu alutambuĩle impola za nkia yaakue; ĩaasio naasĩĩga kĩna witambula impola za kugona ndoolo.
43011014	Paapo ũYesu nuadundulĩla, “uLazalo wakiile.
43011015	Nineene nalumba kunsooko yaani kĩna alĩ nukutilĩ kuasio, koona musuĩĩle; ĩpa kuĩni gua kumuakue.”
43011016	Paapo uTomaso nukuĩtaguaa Tyutĩ, nuaĩĩla ĩamanigua ĩĩa, “Kuĩni nindiisie kukie palumuĩ nduyo.”
43011017	ũYesu pĩna nuuza nuagaana watendile intondo zinĩĩ mukĩbĩĩla.
43011018	ĩBetania alĩ yĩpiipĩ niYelusalemũ, alĩ zĩ maili zibĩlĩ.
43011019	ĩAyahũdi iingĩ alĩ ijile kwa kĩMalita nuMalia, aapumbulie kunsooko ya mugũlĩ waao.
43011020	Paapo uMalita pĩna nũigia ya kĩna ũYesu wapolokaa, numusambĩĩlia, nuMalia nuĩma kukaa.
43011021	Iio uMalita numuĩĩla ũYesu, “Shekulu, kanga ĩalĩĩ ukoolĩ kwanu, umugũlĩ waane sika alĩ wijilikia.
43011022	Ĩpaino manile kĩna luensi kanga umulompe uNzua ukakukupeela.”
43011023	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “uMugũlĩ waako ukiiiuka.”
43011024	uMalita numuĩĩla, “Manile kĩna ukiiiuka muwiiuki palutondo lwa mpelo.”
43011025	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Ĩne neene wiiuki nuupanga; nusuĩlĩĩle mumuane, kanga wakie nakĩ, ukipangata.
43011026	Wensi namupanga nukwishuĩĩla mumuane sika ukikia sunga ĩkalĩ nakalĩ. Usuĩlĩĩlene izi.”
43011027	Numuĩĩla, “Eeze Shekulu, ĩne nasuĩlĩĩle kĩna ue uue Kilisito, uMuana wa kĩNzua, nũjile muna unkũmbigyulu.”
43011028	Pĩna nuzitambula izi nulongola, numuĩta uMalia umunũna waakue kukĩmpisi-mpisi, nuũga, “uMumania ukoolĩ ukukuĩta.”
43011029	Nduyo pĩna nũigia, nuuuka nukaawa, numuagaana.
43011030	nũYesu sika alĩ walapika mukĩsaalĩ, ĩpa alĩ wĩĩlĩ kuuko kĩna uMalita alumuagaanĩĩle.
43011031	ĩAyahũdi naalĩ yĩensi ninduyo munumba kukumupumbulia, pĩna naamuona uMalia wauuka kuukaaũ nukwipũna, naamutiata naishĩĩga kĩna ulunziĩ kukĩbĩĩla walĩle kuasio.
43011032	Iio, uMalia pĩna nupika kuasio kĩna alĩ wĩĩlĩ ũYesu, numuona, nutũngama pamĩgulu yaakue, numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, kanga alĩĩ ukoolĩ kwanu, umugũlĩ wane sika alĩ wijilikia.”
43011033	ũYesu pĩna numuona wilĩla nĩAyahũdi nalĩ ĩtiatile ninduyoo ilĩla, naishululĩla munkolo, nukankanala.
43011034	nuũga, “Mumuĩĩkile mpĩĩ?” Naamuĩĩla, “Shekulu nzuu, ulaae.”
43011035	ũYesu misholi nĩgenda.
43011036	Iio ĩAyahũdi naaũga, “Laaĩ gua kĩna alumuloilue.”
43011037	ĩĨĩa muaasio naaũga, “Uyu naalumulaĩlie ĩmiiso umupokũ, sika wishũũmane kwigilia uyu walekikia?”
43011038	Iio ũYesu naishululĩla kangĩ munkolo, nupika kukĩbĩĩla. Ndĩlo alĩ lyũlũ, nigyũe alĩ yĩĩkue mumulango waakue.
43011039	ũYesu nuũga; “Lĩleegiĩ igyũe.” uMalita, umugũlĩ waakue naalukiile, numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, ĩpa wanũnkaa, kunsooko nantende lutondo lwa kanĩĩ.”
43011040	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Sika aza nukuĩĩlĩĩlene, kanga usuĩĩle ukakuuona uukulu wa kĩNzua?”
43011041	Naalĩleegia igyũe. ũYesu nulangamĩla, nuũga, “Tata, nakusongelagiaa kunsooko wanzigagiaa.
43011042	Nineene manile kĩna ukunzigagiaa intondo tũlũ ĩpa kunsooko ya mulundo naupilimĩkĩlĩĩlĩe ntambuĩle, koona asuĩĩle kĩna uue aluntumile.”
43011043	Pĩna nutambula izi nwĩtunta ululi, “Lazalo pũna, nzuu kunu.”
43011044	Nupũna naalukiile, mutũngue ntiila ĩmĩgulu nĩmĩkono, nuusiu waakue utũngue katiila. ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “Mutũngulĩ, mulekĩ walongole.”
43011045	Iingĩ muAyahũdi naalĩ ijile kwa kĩMalia nukukuziona naaluzitendile ũYesu naasuĩĩla mumuakue.
43011046	ĩĨĩa mumiao naenda kuApalisayo naaaĩĩla naaluzitendile ũYesu. 00284.tif 
 Lindĩ (Yn 11:47)
43011047	Iio, ĩapolia naakulu nĩApalisayo naaĩĩka ilindĩ, naaũga, “Kutendeeii? Kunsooko umuntu uyu witenda ilĩngasĩĩlio iingĩ.
43011048	Kanga kumuleke yoi, tũlũ ensi ikishuĩĩla mumuakue nĩAlumĩ ikiiza, ĩkakukuleegelia ĩnsĩĩ nĩndugu yĩĩtu.”
43011049	Umuĩ waao, uKayafa naalĩ mupolia namukulu umuaka nuasio, nuaĩĩla, “Inie sika mumanile kalukaani,
43011050	sunga sika musĩĩgile kĩna yumũjĩpĩĩle inie muntu umuĩ wakie kunsooko ya antu, ĩndugu yensi ĩlekilimĩĩla.”
43011051	Sika alĩ wĩtambulĩĩle umuene, ĩpa kunsooko alĩ mupolia namukulu umuaka nuasio, nupũnia unakĩdagu kĩna ũYesu ukikia kunsooko ya ndugu;
43011052	kangĩ sika kunsooko ya ndugu ĩĩo udũũ, ĩpa waailingĩĩle ĩaana a kĩNzua naalĩ asapatĩĩle, atũle umuĩ.
43011053	Kwipũna luulo lutondo naakomia ĩkialo amuulage.
43011054	Paapo ũYesu nupela kwiumba tenge-tenge muAyahũdi; iio nulega kuasio nuenda luandĩ piipĩ nĩmbuga kukaa nyukuĩtaguaa Epũlaimu; nwikyala kuuko palumuĩ nĩamanigua aakue.
43011055	nĩPasaka ya Ayahũdi alĩ yĩpiipĩ; iingĩ naanankĩla kwipũna nandĩ zensi kwienda kũYelusalemũ koonna ĩeelie pĩna ĩPasaka alĩ ikaalĩ.
43011056	Paapo naaa kumulaa-laaa ũYesu, naĩkĩtambuĩla eene kueene naĩĩmĩkile muNumba ya kĩNzua, “Musĩĩgileeii? Sika wijilene kulutondo nalukulu?”
43011057	ĩApolia naakulu nĩApalisayo alĩ apũnilie lyagĩĩlio, tũlũ wensi kanga wamane pĩna wĩĩlĩ waleete impola, koona amuguĩle.
43012001	Ntondo mutandatu pĩna alĩ ikĩĩlĩ ĩPasaka, ũYesu nuenda kuBetania pĩna alĩ wĩĩlĩ uLazalo naalumũiukilie kwipũna muakiu.
43012002	Iio naamulũgĩla india za mpĩndĩ kuasio; uMalita nukĩtuma. ULazalo alĩ umuĩ wa aasio naalĩ ĩĩlĩ pandia ensi nduyo.
43012003	Paapo uMalia nuleeta kasali ka makũta ma nalada maaza ma ngele nkakũ, numupaka ũYesu ĩmĩgulu, nupiagula ĩmĩgulu yaakue kumatũmbĩ maakue, nĩnumba nijula ĩnsũla-nsũla ya makũta. 00117.tif 
 Makuta manalada (Yn 12:3)
43012004	ũYuda nwa kuIsikaliote, umuĩ wa amanigua aakue, naalusiile kukumusakia, nuũga,
43012005	“Nĩkĩ ĩmakũta aya masiitigulua kushilinge magana matatu nukwipeegua ĩatũka.”
43012006	Alutambuĩle izi, sika kukuakendegeela ĩatũka, ĩpa kunsooko alĩ mũii, alukuuzaa umĩtĩĩte ĩmbogoosi ya mpeesa, nusola naalĩ iĩĩkue muasio.
43012007	ũYesu nuũga, “Mulekĩ, wamaĩĩkaa aya kulutondo lwa kuĩĩkua kumuane.
43012008	ĩAtũka mwĩensi intondo tũlũ, ĩpa ĩne sika kwĩensi kantondo tũlũ.”
43012009	ĩYũmbĩ kyulu lya Ayahũdi nalĩmana kĩna ukoolĩ kuasio; naaaza, sika kunsooko ya kĩYesu udũũ, ĩpa amuone nuLazalo naalumũiukilie kwipũna muakiu.
43012010	ĩApolia naakulu naakomia ĩkialo amuulage nuLazalo gaa,
43012011	kuitĩ kunsooko yaakue Ayahũdi iingĩ naenda naasuĩĩla mwa kĩYesu.
43012012	Mudaau yaakue iyũmbĩ kyulu lya antu naalĩ ijile kulutondo lukulu pĩna naiigia kĩna ũYesu wijile kũYelusalemũ,
43012013	naazishola ntambĩ za mĩpaama, naapũna kukumusĩngĩĩlia naĩtuntĩkia, Osiana, Wakuligue nũjile muliina lya kĩShekulu, Uuzo Mutemi wa Ĩsilaeli.
43012014	ũYesu pĩna nuona muanandoguĩ, numudaamĩĩla, kĩna yandĩkue,
43012015	“Ulekioopoka munanso Sayuni; Laaa, uMutemi waako wapolokaa Udaamĩlĩĩle muana-ndoguĩ.”
43012016	ĩAmanigua akue sika naazilĩnga izi kumuandio, ĩpa pĩna ũYesu nukuligua, paapo naijuka kĩna alĩ muandĩkĩligue izi, kangĩ kĩna alĩ amutendĩĩle aya.
43012017	Luulo gua, iyũmbi naalĩ yĩensi nduyo nalĩmukuĩla kĩna alumuĩtile uLazalo kwipũna mukĩbĩĩla numũiukia kwipũna muakiu.
43012018	Kunsooko ĩĩo iyũmbĩ nalĩmuagaana, kuitĩ naiigia kĩna alutendile ĩkĩlĩngasĩĩlio ĩkĩ.
43012019	Paapo ĩApalisayo naĩtambuĩla eene kueene, “Laaĩ katĩ, sika musũũmile kakĩntu; uunkũmbigyulu naumutiatĩlĩĩle kunũma yaakue.”
43012020	Alĩ akoolĩ Agiliki muaasio nalĩ anankĩĩle kwienda kukĩtekela kulutondo lukulu.
43012021	Paapo naamuagaana uPilipo nwa kuBetisaida ya Galĩlaya, naamukolia naaũga, “Shekulu, kusiiile kukumuona ũYesu.”
43012022	uPilipo nuenda numuĩĩla uAndelea; uAndelea nuPilipo naenda naamuĩĩla ũYesu.
43012023	ũYesu nuashookeelia nuũga, “iTyũngo liazaa uMuana-muntu wakuligue.
43012024	Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, ĩmpekipemba kanga ĩsiite kwigua munsĩĩ nukwikĩa, ikikyala ing'ene. Kanga ĩkie, yukupĩaa upĩi wingĩ.
43012025	Nuuloilue uuumĩ waakue ukuulimilagia; nuusuukĩĩlue uumĩ waakue muna nkũmbigyulu uu ukuulindĩĩlaa sunga kuupanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ.
43012026	Wensi kanga wantumĩle, nwantiate; pĩna nĩĩlĩ ĩne, paapo numwĩtumi waane ukitũla wĩĩlĩ. Wensi kanga wamtumile, uTata ukakumukulia.
43012027	“Ĩpaino ĩnkolo yaane yakankanalaa, mbũgeeii? Tata, ungũne mutyũngo ĩlĩ. Ĩpa kunsooko ya izi nalĩpikĩĩlaa ityũngo ĩlĩ.
43012028	Tata, kulia ĩliina liako. Paapo naluuza luli kwipũna kwigyulu, Nalĩkulagiaa, kangĩ nĩkakulĩkulia.”
43012029	Iio iyũmbĩ naalĩ liĩmĩkile paasio naigia, naaũga, Yatũla mugũgũmo. ĩĩĩa naaũga, “Malaĩka utambuĩle ninduyo.”
43012030	ũYesu nushookeelia nuũga, “uLuli ulu sika lutũlile kunsooko yaane, ĩpa kunsooko yaani.
43012031	Ĩpaino uulamulua wa unkũmbigyulu uu ukoolĩ; ĩpaino umukulu wa unkũmbigyulu ukitaagua kunzi.
43012032	Nineene pĩna nikinansulua kwipũna muna nsĩĩ, nikilũta tũlũ-tũũlũũ kumuane.”
43012033	Alutambuĩle izi, walagĩĩle nkia kĩ nukikia.
43012034	iYũmbĩ nalĩmushookeelia, “Ishie kũigilie muulagĩĩlio kĩna uKilisito ukikyala sunga ĩkalĩ nakalĩ, ninduue waũga mbii kĩna ijipĩĩle uMuana-muntu wanansulue. uMuana-muntu uyu waani?”
43012035	Iio ũYesu nuaĩĩla, “uWeelu kĩlĩ ukoolĩ kumiani tyũngo; mugende pĩna mutĩĩte uweelu, ĩkiitĩ kĩleke kumuguĩla. Nukugendalaa mukiiti sika wĩĩzĩ kĩna ulunziĩ.
43012036	Pĩna mutĩĩte uweelu suĩĩlĩ muweelu, mutũle aana a weelu.” Pĩna nutambula izi ũYesu, nulega kwipũna kumiao nwĩpisa.
43012037	Kanga alutendile ilĩngasĩĩlio iingĩ nakĩ ntongela yaao, sika naasuĩĩla mumuakue,
43012038	koona lutimĩĩligue ulukaani lwa kĩYesaya umunakĩdagu naalutambuĩle, “Shekulu, waani nusuĩlĩĩle impola zĩtu. Numukono wa kĩShekulu alĩ mukũnukulĩlue waani?”
43012039	Kunsooko ĩĩ sika naasũũma kwishuĩĩla, kuitĩ uYesaya nuũga kangĩ,
43012040	“Uapokũilie ĩmiiso, Uakakĩĩlie inkolo Alekiona namiiso maao, Alekilĩnga munkolo zaao, Agomoke, nĩakamie.”
43012041	uYesaya aluũgile izi pĩna aluoonie uukulu waakue, nutambula impola zaakue.
43012042	Ĩpa sunga muakulu alĩ akoolĩ iingĩ naasuĩlĩĩle mumuakue, ĩpa kunsooko ya Apalisayo sika naakũmuula, alekikamatulua mũshũnagogi.
43012043	Kuitĩ alĩ aloogue ulukumo lwa antu kwikĩla ulukũmo lwa kĩNzua.
43012044	ũYesu nwĩtunta ululi nuũga, “Nusuĩlĩĩle mumuane sikunsuĩlĩĩle kaneene, ĩpa uuyo naaluntumile.
43012045	Nundaaile ĩne amulaaile naaluntumile.
43012046	Ĩne nijile nĩĩ weelu muna unkũmbigyulu, koona tũlũ wensi nusũlĩĩle mumuane waleke kikyala mukiiti.
43012047	Wensi kanga wiigie inkaani zaane kanga waleke kuzikendegeela, ĩne sika nukumulamula, kunsooko sika nijile nuulamule uunkũmbigyulu, ĩpa nuugũne uunkũmbigyulu.
43012048	Nwakunsiita ĩne, nasikukuanũnkulaa inkaani zaane, utĩĩte nwakumulamula; ulukaani nanulutambuĩle, luulo lukakumulamula palutondo lwa mpelo.
43012049	Kunsooko sika alĩ ntambuĩle ning'ene, ĩpa uTata naaluntumile, muene undagĩlĩĩlie nanikiũga nikwitambula.
43012050	Nineene manile kĩna ilyagĩĩlio liakue ingĩ upanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ. Izi nanukutambulaa gua; kĩna uTata alumbuĩlĩĩle, iio nukutambulaa.”
43013001	uLutondo lukulu lwa Pasaka pĩna alĩ lwikaalĩ ũYesu numanile kĩna ityũngo liakue liazaaa lya kulega muna unkũmbigyulu uu wende kwa kĩTata, alĩ ualoilue ĩaakue muna unkũmbigyulu, nualoogua sunga kumpelo.
43013002	Pĩna alĩ ilĩa india za mpĩndĩ, ũShetani nwakondilie kwiingĩlia ĩmasĩĩgo munkolo ya kĩYuda ũsha Simoni nwa kuIsikaliote kukumusakia.
43013003	Luulo gua, ũYesu numanile kĩna uTata alĩ wamupĩĩle tũlũ mumĩkono yaakue nĩkangĩ kĩna alupũnile kwa kĩNzua nukwilongola kwa kĩNzua,
43013004	nuuuka pandia, nuĩĩka luandĩ intiila zaakue, nusola kĩdeeo nwĩtũnga.
43013005	Pembele nutaagĩla ĩmaazĩ mukĩĩko nuandia kukuakalalia ĩamanigua ĩmĩgulu nukwipiagula nakĩdeeo naalĩ wĩtungile.
43013006	Paapo nupika pa kĩSimoni Petelo. uNuasio numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, ue winkalaliane ĩmĩgulu?”
43013007	ũYesu nushookeelia numuĩĩla, “Nanitenda ĩne sika umanile ĩpaino; pembele ukilĩnga.”
43013008	uPetelo numuĩĩla, “Sika ukinkalalia ĩmĩgulu yaane sunga ĩkalĩ nakalĩ.” ũYesu numushookeelia, “Kanga nsiite kukukalalia, sika kwityũmpĩ palumuĩ nineene.”
43013009	uSimoni Petelo numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, sika kamĩgulu yaane udũũ, sunga nĩmĩkono nityũe gaa.”
43013010	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “uNuasio noogile ukukalalaa ĩmĩgulu udũũ, ĩpa umuĩlĩ wensi muelu, niniinie muelile, ĩpa sika tũlũ ensi.”
43013011	Kuitĩ alumumanile nukakumusakia; luulo nuũga, “Sika mwĩeelu tũlũ ensi.”
43013012	Pĩna nukondia kukuakalalia ĩmĩgulu, nusola intiila zaakue, nwikyalansa kangĩ pandia, nuaĩĩla, “Mwalĩngane naaza numutendĩĩle?
43013013	Ĩnie mwinjĩta Mumaania kangĩ Shekulu; Mwitambula iiza, ingĩ neene.
43013014	Kanga uneene naniShekulu kangĩ Mumania namukalalia ĩmĩgulu, ijĩpĩĩle niniinie kukĩkalalia ĩmĩgulu.
43013015	Kuitĩ numupĩĩle mpiani; kĩna numutendĩĩle inie, niniinie mutende iio-iioo.
43013016	Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, uMusese sika mukulu kwikĩla ũShekulu waakue, katia umutumua sika mukulu kwikĩla numutumile.
43013017	Kanga mumane zaasio, mualiukũ kanga muzitende.
43013018	Sika nitambula impola zaani inie tũlũ. Nĩĩĩzĩ nanĩasaaguĩle, ĩpa uwandĩkua utimĩĩligue, Nulĩĩle india zaane nunsamba ilyakĩ.
43013019	Kwipũna ĩpaino namuĩĩla pĩna ikaalĩ kukigyelela, koona pĩna ikigyelela musuĩĩle kĩna ingĩ neene.
43013020	Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, uNuasio nukumuanũnkula wensi nanumutumile ukunanũnkulaa uneene; nduyo nukunanũnkulaa ĩne ukumuanũnkulaa uzo naaluntumile.”
43013021	Pĩna nutambula izi, ũYesu nukankanala munkolo nukuĩla nuũga, “Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, umuĩ waani ukinshakia.”
43013022	ĩAmanigua naĩlaa, naiiona nkankani, waani gile nukumugamba.
43013023	Alukoolĩ umuĩ wa amanigua aakue naalumuegamĩĩle ũYesu mukĩkũa kiakue, uzo ũYesu naalumuloilue.
43013024	Iio uSimoni Petelo numuangaazĩlia umukono, numuĩĩla, “Mukolie waani nukumugamba.”
43013025	uNuasio pĩna alumuegamĩĩle ũYesu mukĩkũa kiakue, numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, waani gile.”
43013026	Paapo ũYesu nushookeelia, “Ingĩ uuyo nanĩkakumulĩĩlĩlia ĩntonge nukukumupeela.” Numĩlĩĩlia ĩntonge, numupeela ũYuda ũsha Simoni nwa kuIsikaliote.
43013027	Pĩna numĩlia ĩntonge, paapo ũShetani numũingĩĩla, ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Kĩna witenda, tendaanga.”
43013028	Alukutili muaasio naalĩ ikyalansile pandia naalumanile kunsooko kĩ ukumuĩĩla itĩ.
43013029	ĩĨĩa, kunsooko ũYuda alumĩtĩĩte ĩmbogoosi ya mpeesa, naasĩĩga kĩna ũYesu alumuĩĩlĩĩle, “Gula nakuasilĩlue kulutondo nalukulu,” katia waapeele ĩatũka kĩntu.
43013030	Paapo unuasio pĩna numianũnkula ĩntonge, ĩkamuĩ nupũna; alĩ utiku.
43013031	Pĩna nupũna, ũYesu nuũga, “Ĩpaino wakulagiguaa uMuana-muntu, nuNzua wakulagiguaa mumuakue.
43013032	uNzua kanga wakuligue mumuakue, uNzua ukakumukulia munsĩ yaakue; ĩkamuĩ ukakumukulia.
43013033	Aana aane namuaniino, kĩlĩ nkoolĩ tyungo niino palumuĩ niniinie. Mukindaaa-laa-la; kĩna alĩ nĩaĩĩlĩĩle ĩAyahũdi, ĩpaino namuĩĩla niniinie, ĩne, kĩna nunziĩ, inie sika mwishũũma kwiiiza.
43013034	Namupeela lyagĩĩlio nĩpia, mwĩloogue. Kĩnaalĩ numuloilue inie, niniinie mwĩloogue iio-iioo.
43013035	Kuitĩ tũlũ ikilĩnga kĩna inie mwĩamanigua aane, kanga muĩ nuuloogua niinie kuniinie.”
43013036	uSimoni Petelo numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, ulunziĩ mpĩĩ?” ũYesu nushookeelia, “Kĩna nunziĩ ĩne, sika wishũũma kwintiata ĩpaino; ukintiata pembele.”
43013037	uPetelo numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, nĩkĩ sika nishũũma kukutiata ĩpaino? Nikipũnia uumĩ waane kunsooko yaako.”
43013038	ũYesu nushookeelia; Ukĩpũniane uuumĩ waako kunsooko yaane. Tai-taaii nakuĩĩla, uMumbĩ sika ukikunkula pina uwe ukawankana nkua zitatu.
43014001	“ĩNkolo zaani zilekikankanala; musuĩĩle mwa kĩNzua, musuĩĩle numumuane.
43014002	Munumba mwa kĩTata waane ukoolĩ wikyalo wingĩ; kanga ĩsika iio, aza nijilekumuĩĩla. Nalongola kukumuzĩpĩlĩĩlia uwĩĩmo.
43014003	Pĩna nalongola kukumuzipilĩĩlia uwĩĩmo, nikiiiza kangĩ numuanũnkule kumuane, koona pĩna nĩĩlĩ ĩne, niniinie muĩ paapo.
43014004	Kĩna nunziĩ mumĩmanile ĩnzĩla.”
43014005	uTomaso numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, sika kumanile kĩna ulunziĩ, kukakumĩmana mbii ĩnzĩla?”
43014006	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Ĩne neene nzĩla nĩtai nuupanga; ukutilĩ nũjile kwa kĩTata isiititũla kunzĩla ya ĩne.
43014007	Kanga ĩalĩĩ munĩngile ĩne alĩ mũjile kumulĩnga nuTata. Kwipũna ĩpaino mwamulĩngaa, kangĩ mwamuonaa.”
43014008	uPilipo numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, kulagĩĩle uTata, koona yakuenda muumo.”
43014009	ũYesu numuĩĩla, “Ĩne nikyalikilie nakwĩensi niniinie, sikunĩngilene Pilipo? Numoonie ĩne wamuoonie nuTata. Wiũgaaii ue, kulagĩĩle uTata.
43014010	Sika wishuĩĩlane kĩna ĩne moolĩ mwa kĩTata, nuTata umoolĩ mumuane. iNkaani nanukumuĩĩla ĩne sika nĩkĩtambulĩlagiaa ning'ene, ĩpa uTata nũkyalile munsĩ yaane ukĩtumaa ĩmĩlĩmo yaakue.
43014011	Nsuĩĩlĩ kĩna ĩne nkoolĩ mwa kĩTata nuTata ukoolĩ mumuane; naa sika iio, nsuĩĩlĩ kunsooko ya mĩlĩmo ĩmiene.
43014012	“Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, nusuĩlĩĩle mumuane, ĩmĩlĩmo nanĩkĩtuma ĩne nduzo ukakuĩtuma, kangĩ namĩkulu kwikĩla ĩĩ ukakĩtuma kunsooko nalongolaa kwa kĩTata.
43014013	Luensi namukakululompa muliina liane nĩkakulutenda, uTata wakuligue muMuana.
43014014	Luensi kanga munompe muliina liane nĩkakulutenda.”
43014015	Kanga mundoogue mukikendegeela ĩmalagĩĩlio maane.
43014016	Nineene nĩkakumulompa uTata, nduzo ukakumupeela Mualĩĩlia numuua, wikyale niniinie ĩkalĩ nakalĩ;
43014017	uMuau nwa tai; uunkũmbigyulu sika wishũũma kukumuanũnkula kunsooko sika umuoonie, sunga sika umulĩngile. Ĩnie mumulĩngile kunsooko wikyalile kumuani, nduzo ukitũla munsĩ yaani.
43014018	“Sika nĩkakumuleka inie mwĩakĩa; nijile kumiani.
43014019	Kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino uunkũmbigyulu sika wimona kangĩ, ĩpa inie mwĩmona kunsooko ĩne numupamga, niniinie mukitũla muapanga.
43014020	Palutondo luasio mukimana uniniie kĩna ĩne moolĩ mwa kĩTata waane, niniinie mumoolĩ mumuane nineene moolĩ mumiani.
43014021	uNuasio nutĩĩte ĩmalagĩĩlio maane nukukumakendegeela, unuasio undoilue; nduzo nundoilue ukiloogua nuTata waane, nineene nĩkakumuloogua nukukigyelela kumuakue.”
43014022	ũYuda, (sika nwa kuIsikaliote,) numuĩĩla, “Shekulu, ikitũla mbii kĩna usiiile kukigyelela kumuĩtu, sika kuunkũmbigyulu?”
43014023	ũYesu nushookeelia numuĩĩla, “Wensi kanga wandoogue ukikendegeela ulukaani luane, nuTata waane ukakumuloogua, nindiishie kukiiiza kumuakue nukwitenda wikyalo kumuakue.
43014024	Nasika undoulue sikukukendegeelaa inkaani zaane, nulukaani namukulũigagiaa sika luane, ingĩ lwa kĩTata naaluntumile.
43014025	“Izi alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle pĩna alĩ kuuzaa nkoolĩ kumiani.
43014026	Ĩpa uMualĩĩlia, uMuau Muelu, uTata nukakumutuma muliina liane, unuasio ukakumumania tũlũ zensi nukukumũjukĩlia tũlũ zensi naalĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle.
43014027	ĩMatiliga namulekela; ĩmatiliga maane namupeela, ĩne nukumupeelaa sika kĩna uunkũmbigyulu naukumupeelaa. iNkolo zaani zilekikankanala sunga zilekiopoka.
43014028	“Mũigilie kĩna ĩne alĩnumuĩlĩĩle kĩna nalongola, nijile kangĩ kumiani. Kanga ĩalĩĩ mundoilue alĩ mũjililumba kunsooko nalongola kwa kĩTata, kuitĩ uTata ingĩ mukulu kwikĩla ĩne.
43014029	Nĩndĩĩpa numuĩĩlĩĩle pĩna ikaali kukigyela, koona pĩna ĩkakigyelela, musuĩĩle.
43014030	Sika nĩkakumutambuĩla ningĩ kangĩ kunsooko umukulu wa unkũmbigyulu wapolokaa. Mugila kakĩntu kumuane;
43014031	ĩpa uunkũmbigyulu umane kĩna numuloilue uTata, iio nukutendaa kĩna uTata alundagĩlĩĩlie. Uukĩ kwĩĩni kulege kunu.”
43015001	“Ĩne neene muzabiibu wa tai, nuTata waane ingĩ mulĩmi.
43015002	uLutambĩ luensi munsĩ yaane nasika lukupĩaa inkali ukululeegagiaa; luensi nalukupĩaa ukulusogolelaa koona lupĩĩkie inkali ningĩ.
43015003	Ĩnie ĩpaino mwieelu kunsooko ya lukaani naalĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle.
43015004	Kyalĩ munsĩ yaane, nineene munsĩ yaani. Kĩna ulutambĩ nasika lusũũmile kwipĩa lwing'ene kanga lusiite kukikyala mumukali, iio niniinie kanga musiite kukikyala munsĩ yaane.
43015005	Ĩne neene muzabiibu, inie mwĩntambĩ. Nwikyalile munsĩ yaane nineene munsĩ yaakue, ukupĩĩkagiaa. Kanga ĩsika neene sika mwishũũma kwitenda kalukaani.
43015006	Wensi kanga wasiite kukikyala munsĩ yaane, ukutaagaguaa kunzi zĩ lutambĩ nukwiuuma; nintambĩ zukuilingĩĩlagua nukwitaagua mumooto, nazishonsua.
43015007	Kanga mwikyale munsĩ yaane ninkaani zaane zikyale munsĩ yaani, lompĩ luensi namusiiile, mukitendelua.
43015008	Iio uTata waane ukukulagiguaa, pĩna mukupĩaa inkali naningĩ; niniinie mukitũla amanigua aane.
43015009	“Kĩna uTata naalundoilue ĩne, iio nineene numuloilue inie; kyalĩ muuloogua waane.
43015010	Kanga mukendegeele ĩmalagĩĩlio maane, mukakikyala muuloogua waane, kĩna uneene naalĩ nĩmakendegelĩĩle ĩmalagĩĩlio ma kĩTata waane, nanikyala muuloogua waakue.
43015011	Izi alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle, uulumbi waane wikyale munsĩ yaani nuulumbi waani utimĩĩligue.
43015012	“iLyagĩĩlio liane ntĩĩli, mwiloogue kĩna alĩ numuloilue inie.
43015013	Ukutilĩ nutĩĩte uloogua naukulu kwikĩla uu, umuntu wapũnie uuumĩ waakue kunsooko ya asuaĩĩa.
43015014	Inie mwĩasuaĩaane kanga mutende nanumulagĩlĩĩlie.
43015015	Sika nukumuĩta kangĩ asese, kunsooko umusese sika wĩĩzĩ kĩna ukutendaa ũshekulu waakue. Ĩnie numuĩtile asuaĩaane, kunsooko tũlũ zensi nanĩziigilie kwa kĩTata nukumulĩngagiaa.
43015016	Inie sika alĩ munsaaguĩle ĩne, ĩpa neene alĩ numusaaguĩle inie, nanumuĩĩka muende mupĩe inkali, ninkali zaani zikyale; koona luensi kanga mumulompe uTata muliina liane wamupeele.
43015017	Izi nukumulagĩĩlia koona mwĩloogue.”
43015018	“Kanga uunkũmbigyulu umusuukĩlue inie, mulĩnge kĩna ĩne neene namuandio kwishuukĩlua nduo.
43015019	Kanga ĩazaa mwa unkũmbigyulu, uunkũmbigyulu aza wijile kualoogua ĩaakue; ĩpa kunsooko inie sika mwa unkũmbigyulu, ĩpa ĩne alĩ numusaaguĩle inie muunkũmbigyulu, iio gua, uunkũmbigyulu ukumusuukĩlaguaa.
43015020	Lũjukĩ ulukaani naalĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle, musese sika mukulu kwikĩla ũshekulu waakue. Malĩĩ alĩĩ anzagilie ĩne, ĩkakumuagia niniinie. Malĩĩ alĩĩ alukendegelĩĩle ulukaani luane, ĩkakulukendegeela nulukaani luani.
43015021	Ĩpa izi tũlũ ĩkakumutendela kunsooko ya liina liane, kuitĩ sika amuĩzĩ naaluntumile.
43015022	Kanga alĩ nsiitiiiza nukukuatambuĩla ĩo, sika alĩ ijilitũla numulandu ĩpa agila kawĩlongo kumulandu waao.
43015023	Nukunsuukĩlaguaa ĩne, ukumusuukĩlaguaa nuTata waane.
43015024	Kanga alĩ nsiite kukĩtuma ĩmĩlĩmo kumiao nasika alĩ witumile nuĩngĩ, sika alĩ ijilitũla numulandu, ĩpa akuonaa nukukukusuukĩlua ĩne nuTata waane gaa.
43015025	Ĩpa lutimĩĩligue ulukaani naalĩ luandĩkue muUlagĩĩlio waao, Alĩ ansuukĩlue nakanda.
43015026	Ĩpa pĩna waaza uMualĩĩlia nanĩkakumutuma ĩne kwipũna kwa kĩTata, uMuau nwa tai nupũnile kwa kĩTata, unuasio ukinkuĩla;
43015027	niniinie gaa mukunkuĩlaa, kunsooko kwipũna umuandio alĩ kwĩensi nineene.”
43016001	“Izi alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle mulekikũmpigua.
43016002	Ĩkakumukamatula mumasũnagogi; ĩtai ityũngo lijile, wensi kanga wamuulage inie ukishĩĩga ukumutumĩla uNzua.
43016003	Nindiizi ĩkakuzitenda kunsooko sika alĩ amuĩzĩ uTata sunga uneene.
43016004	Ĩpa alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle koona ityũngo liao pĩna likiiiza muzijuke kĩna ĩne alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle. Izi sika alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle kwipũna umuandio kunsooko alĩ kwĩensi niniinie.
43016005	Ĩpaino nalongola kumuakue naaluntumile. Ukutilĩ mumuani nwinkolia, Ulunziĩ mpĩĩ?
43016006	Ĩpa kunsooko naalĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle izi, uusungu wijula inkolo zaani.
43016007	Ĩpa ĩne namuĩĩla ĩtai, yumũjĩpĩle inie ĩne ndege; kuitĩ kanga nsiitilega, uMualĩĩlia sika wijile kumiani; ĩpa kanga nende nĩkakumutuma kumuani.
43016008	Na waaza unuasio ukakuusokia uunkũmbigyulu kumpola za mulandu nĩkulukuuluu nuulamuli.
43016009	Kumpola za mulandu, kunsooko sika asuĩlĩĩle mumuane.
43016010	Kumpola za kulukuuluu, kunsooko nalongolaa kwa kĩTata; sika mwimona kangĩ.
43016011	Kumpola za ulamuli kunsooko umukulu wa unkũmbigyulu uu walamulaguaa.”
43016012	“Kĩlĩ ntĩĩte ningĩ za kumuĩĩla, ĩpa sika mwishũũma kukuzigigimĩlia ĩpaino.
43016013	Ĩpa pĩna ukiiiza unuasio, uMuau nwa tai, ukakumutongeela inie mutai tũlũ yensĩ, kunsooko sika ukakĩtambulĩlia wing'ene, ĩpa ziizo nukakuziigia ukitambula; sunga nazijile ukakumutanantĩlia.
43016014	uNuasio ukinkulia ĩne, kunsooko ukishola ĩzaane nukakumutanantĩlia inie.
43016015	Tũlũ zensi nutĩĩte uTata ingĩ zaaane, luulo alĩ ntambuĩle kĩna ukusolaa ĩzaane nukukumutanantĩlia.
43016016	“Kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino sika mwimona; kangĩ kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino mukimona.”
43016017	Paapo ityũmpi lya amanigua naĩtambuĩla eene kueene. “Yaani itĩ nukukuĩĩla, kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino sika mwimona, kangĩ kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino mukimona; kangĩ, Kunsooko nalongola kwa kĩTata?”
43016018	Iio naaũga, “Yaani itĩ nwiũga, Kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino. Sika kumanile witambula yaani.”
43016019	ũYesu nulĩnga kĩna asiiile kukumukolia, nuaĩĩla, “Mukĩkoliane naaza mbũgile, kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino sika mwimona, kangĩ kĩlĩ katũngo kaniino mukimona?
43016020	Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, mukikuuta kĩlĩlo nukwilĩla inie, ĩpa uunkũmbigyulu ukilumba; inie mukileetelua usungu, ĩpa uusungu waani ukikaĩlĩka wĩĩ ulumbi.
43016021	Umusungu pĩna wĩkĩtũnguĩla utĩĩte uusungu kunsooko ityũngo liakue liazaa; pĩna wamulela umuana, sika ukulũjuka kangĩ uluago kunsooko ya ulumbi wa kalelua umuntu muna unkũmbigyulu.
43016022	Iio niniinie mutĩĩte uusungu ĩpaino, ĩpa nĩkakumuona kangĩ ninkolo zaani zikilumba, nuulumbi waani ukutilĩ nukumuleegelia.
43016023	Mulutondo luasio sika mukinkolia kalukaani. Tai-taaii namuĩĩla, luensi kanga mumulompe uTata muliina liane ukakumupeela.
43016024	Sunga ĩpaino sika mulompile kalukaani muliina liane. Lompĩ, mukiligia, uulumbi waani wĩĩ ukamĩnkĩĩlũ.
43016025	“Izi numuĩĩlĩĩle inie kuung'enua; ityũngo lijile sika nikitambula niniinie kangĩ kuung'enua, ĩpa nĩkakumudundulĩla impola za kĩTata.
43016026	Palutondo luasio mukilompa muliina liane; sika nukumuĩĩla kĩna nĩkakumulompeela inie kwa kĩTata.
43016027	Kunsooko uTata muene umuloilue inie, kuitĩ inie mwandoilue nukwishuĩĩla kĩna ĩne alĩ mpũnile kwa kĩTata.
43016028	Alĩ mpũnile kwa kĩTata, naazile muna unkũmbigyulu; kangĩ naulekaa uunkũmbigyulu, nalongolaa kwa kĩTata.”
43016029	ĩAmanigua aakue naaũga, “Laaa gua, ĩpaino witambula tengetenge, sikakawitambula kuung'enua.
43016030	Ĩpaino kumanile kĩna umanile tũlũ-tũũlũũ, sika wishiia tũlũ wensi wakukolie; luulo kwasuĩĩla kĩna ue upũnile kwa kĩNzua.”
43016031	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Iino mwasuĩĩlane.
43016032	Laaa gua, ityũngo lijile, kangĩ liazaa, mukishapatĩla muntu wensi kunsiao, mukindeka ning'ene. ĩpa sika ning'ene, kunsooko uTata ukoolĩ palumuĩ nineene.
43016033	Izi alĩ numuĩĩlĩĩle muĩ nĩmatiliga mumuane. Muna unkũmbigyulu mutĩĩte luago ĩpa kamiĩ nkolo; ĩne naudulile uunkũmbigyulu.”
43017001	iNkaani izi aluzitambuĩle ũYesu; nulangamĩla kwigyulu, nuũga, “Tata, ityũngo liazaa. Kulia ue uMuana waako, koona uMuana wakukulie ue,
43017002	kĩna yoi naalumupĩĩle uusũũmi kuensi naakola muĩlĩ, itĩ tũlũ naalumupĩĩle waapeele uupanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ.
43017003	Nuupanga wa kalĩ nakalĩ ingĩ ntuuu, akumane ue nwĩNzua nwing'ene nwa tai, nũYesu Kilisito nalumutumile.
43017004	Ĩne alĩ nukukulĩlie muna nsĩĩ; nanuumalĩĩlia umulĩmo naalumpĩĩle nuutume.
43017005	Ĩpaino Tata, nkulia pamuako kuukulu waasio naalĩ ntĩĩte kumuako pĩna uunkũmbigyulu alĩ wikaalĩ.
43017006	“ĩLiina liako naligyelelagiaa kuantu naalumpĩĩle muna unkũmbigyulu. Alĩ aako, numpeela ĩne, nulukaani luako alukendegeelaa.
43017007	Ĩpaino amanile kĩna tũlũ zensi naalumpĩĩle zipũnile kumuako.
43017008	Kunsooko inkaani naalumpĩĩle ĩne naapĩĩle; naazaanũnkula, naamana ĩtai kĩna mpũnile kumuako; naasuĩĩla kĩna uue aluntumile.
43017009	Ĩne nukualompeela ĩa, sika nukuulompeela uunkũmbigyulu, ĩpa aao nalumpĩĩle, kunsooko ingĩ aako.
43017010	Tũlũ zensi naalĩ zaane ingĩ zaako; nĩzaako ingĩ zaane; nineene nakulagiguaa munsĩ yaao.
43017011	“Nineene sika nkoolĩ muna unkũmbigyulu; ĩa akoolĩ muna unkũmbigyulu, nineene naazaa kumuako. Tata numuelu, uakendegeele muliina liako aao naalumpĩĩle, koona atũle, umuĩ zĩ undiishie.
43017012	Pĩna alĩ kwĩensi ĩne alĩ nĩakendegelĩĩle muliina liako; aao naalumpĩĩle alĩ nĩalindĩlĩĩle, ukutilĩ nunumuĩ mumuao naalulimĩlĩĩle ĩpa umuana wa ulimĩĩli, uwandĩkua utimĩĩligue.
43017013	Ĩpaino nijile kumuako, nindiizi nazitambulaa muna unkũmbigyulu koona uulumbi waane utimĩĩligue munsĩ yaao.
43017014	Ĩne naapĩĩle ulukaani luako, nuunkũmbigyulu waasuukĩĩlue kunsooko ĩa sika a unkũmbigyulu kĩna uneene nasika na unkũmbigyulu.
43017015	Sika nilompa ualeegie muna unkũmbigyulu, ĩpa uakendegeele kumubĩĩ.
43017016	Ĩa sika a unkũmbigyulu kĩna uneene nasika na unkũmbigyulu.
43017017	Ueelie mutai, ulukaani luako ingĩ tai.
43017018	Kĩna iio naaluntumile muna unkũmbigyulu, nineene iio nĩatumile muna unkũmbigyulu.
43017019	Nukunsooko yaao nĩeelagiaa, koona nĩndĩo eeligue mutai.
43017020	“Sika nukualompeela awa dũũ, ĩpa nĩndĩĩo naikishuĩĩla mumuane kunsooko ya lukaani luao
43017021	Tũlũ ensi atũle umuĩ kĩna ue Tata nukoolĩ mumuane nineene moolĩ mumuako, koona ĩa atũle umuĩ munsĩ yĩĩtu, uunkũmbigyulu usuĩĩle kĩna uue untumile.
43017022	Nineene, uukulu naalumpĩĩle ĩne, naapeelaa awa, atũle umuĩ zĩ undiishie.
43017023	Ĩne munsĩ yaao nunduue munsi yaane, koona atũle akamatĩkũ muumuĩ, uunkũmbigyulu umane kĩna uue alutumile, nualoogua ĩa kĩna alundoilue ĩne.
43017024	“Tata, ĩaasio nwampĩĩle ĩne, nsiiile ĩĩ palumuĩ nineene pĩna nĩĩlĩ, alaae uukulu waane nwampĩĩle ĩne, kunsooko alundoilue pĩna umukulĩla wa unkũmbigyulu alĩ wikaalĩ kalaĩĩkua
43017025	Tata mukola kulukuuluu, uunkĩmbigyulu sika ukumanile ue, ĩpa ĩne nukumanile ue, nĩndĩĩa amanile kĩna uue alutumile.
43017026	Naamanilie ĩliina liako, kangĩ nĩkakuamania; itĩ uuloogua naalundoilue ĩne wĩĩ munsĩ yaao, nineene nĩĩ munsĩ yaao.”
43018001	Pĩna nutambula izi, ũYesu nupũna palumuĩ nĩamanigua aakue, nulongola kwityumbĩ lya kamongo Kidoloni pĩna alĩ kĩtanga. Nũingĩla muumo umuene nĩamanigua aakue.
43018002	NũYuda, umusakia waakue, alĩ wĩĩzĩ paasio kunsooko ũYesu nĩamanigua aakue alĩ akĩlundĩĩlaa paasio nkua kunkua.
43018003	Luulo, ũYuda pĩna nuligia ĩkĩũmbĩ kya ĩlaasi nĩĩtumi a apolia naakulu nĩApalisayo, nuenda kuasio niimulĩ nintala nĩmata.
43018004	Iio ũYesu kunsooko alumanile tũlũ nazĩkakumuagaana, nupũna nuaĩĩla, “Mukumudũũma waani?”
43018005	Naamushookeelia, “ũYesu Munazaleti.” Nuaĩĩla, “Ingĩ neene.” ũYuda, umusakia waakue, aluĩmĩkile palumuĩ nĩndĩo.
43018006	Pĩna nuaĩĩla, “Ingĩ neene,” naashooka kĩnũũma naagua pansĩ.
43018007	Nuakolia kaubĩlĩ, “Mukumudũũma waani.” Naaũga, “ũYesu Munazaleti.”
43018008	ũYesu nuashookeelia, “Nuaĩĩla kĩna ingĩ neene. Malĩĩ mwindũũma ĩne, alekĩ ĩa ende.”
43018009	koona lutimĩĩligue ulukaani nalutambulue, “Ĩa naalumpĩĩle sika alĩ nĩalimĩlĩĩlie kaumuĩ.”
43018010	Paapo uSimoni Petelo, naalutĩĩte iyũmba, nulĩsopoola numutema umusese wa mupolia namukulu, numudumula ukutũi wa kĩgoosia. ĩLiina lya musese alĩ Malikusi.
43018011	Paapo ũYesu numuĩĩla uPetelo, “Shookeelia iyũmba mukĩnina. ĩKĩĩko numpĩĩle uTata, nsiite kukĩkopelane?”
43018012	Paapo ĩkĩũmbi kya ĩlaasi numukulu waao nĩĩtumi a Ayahũdi naamuguĩla ũYesu naamutũnga,
43018013	naamulongolia tangua kwa kĩAnasi, kunsooko alĩ mukuĩ wa kĩKayapa naalĩ mupolia namukulu umuaka nuasio.
43018014	nuKayapa muene aluapĩĩle ĩAyahũdi ĩkialo kĩna ijĩpĩĩle muntu umuĩ wakie kunsooko ya antu.
43018015	uSimoni Petelo numutiata ũYesu, numumanigua nuĩngĩ. uMumanigua nuasio alĩ mumanue numupolia namukuluu, nũingĩla palumuĩ nũYesu mukĩanda kya mupolia namukulu.
43018016	Ĩpa uPetelo nuĩmĩka kunzi pamulango. Iio umumanigua nuasio nuĩngĩ naalĩ mumanue numupolia namukulu nupũna, naĩtambuĩla numulindĩĩla-mulango, numũingĩlia uPetelo.
43018017	Paapo ĩkatũgua kalindĩĩla-mulango nakamuĩĩla uPetelo, “Sika uene umuĩ wa amanigua a muntu uyo?” uNuasio nuũga, “Ĩne sikaka neene.”
43018018	ĩAsese nĩĩtumi alĩ ĩĩmĩkile naikoleelia umooto wa makala naioota kunsooko alĩ mpepo. uPetelo alĩ yĩensi palumuĩ ndĩo, nuĩmĩkile nwioota umooto.
43018019	Paapo umupolia namukulu numukolia ũYesu impola za amanigua aakue nimpola za umania waakue.
43018020	ũYesu nushookeelia, “Ĩne alĩ ntambuĩle tengetenge muna unkũmbigyulu; ĩne intondo tũlũ nukumanagiaa mũshũnagogi numuNumba ya kĩNzua pĩna ĩkĩlundĩĩlĩĩlaa ĩAyahũdi tũlũ; sika ntambuĩle kalukaani kukĩmpisĩ-mpisĩ.
43018021	Nĩkĩ winkolia ĩne. Akolie naalĩ akũigagiaa naalĩ nukuaĩĩlaa. Laaa, ĩo amanile naalĩ nukuzitambula ĩne.”
43018022	Pĩna nutambula izi umuĩ wa ĩtumi naaluĩmĩkile paasio numukua ũYesu lupĩĩ, nuũga, “Iione ukumushookeelia umupolia namukulu?”
43018023	ũYesu numushookeelia, “Kanga ĩntambuĩle ibĩĩ, ukuĩle uubĩĩ waasio; kanga iiza, wankua nĩkĩ?”
43018024	Paapo uAnasi numutuala mutũngue kwa kĩKayapa umupolia namukulu.
43018025	NuSimoni Petelo alĩ wĩĩmĩkile nwioota umooto. Naamuĩĩla, “Sika uuene umuĩ wa amanigua aakue?” Uyu nukaana nuũga, “Sikaka neene.”
43018026	Umuĩ wa asese a mupolia namukulu, muntua wa kĩnuasio naalĩ mudumulue ukutuĩ nuPetelo, nuũga, “Ĩne sika aza nukuooniene mukĩtanga mwĩensi nduyo?”
43018027	Paapo uPetelo nukaana kangĩ; ĩkamuĩ umumbĩ nukunkula.
43018028	Paapo naamupũnia ũYesu kwa kĩKayapa, naamutuala kwijumba lya kĩtemi mũgyĩngu. Io sika alĩ ingĩĩle mwijumba lya kĩtemi, alekipũũta umũiko, ĩpa alĩe ĩnkolo ya Pasaka.
43018029	Paapo uPilatu nupũna kunzi nuũga, “Muleetile usokia kĩ kumuntu uzu.”
43018030	Naashookeelia naamuĩĩla, “Kanga uyu ĩsika mutenda ibĩĩ sika aza kumuleetile kumuako.”
43018031	Iio uPilatu nuaĩĩla, “Musolĩ uniinie mumulamule kuUlagĩĩlio waani.” ĩAyahũdi naamushookeelia, “Kuasiitĩligue ishie kukumuulaga umuntu.”
43018032	Itĩ ulukaani lwa kĩYesu lutimĩĩligue naalutambuĩle, nalagĩĩla nkia kĩ nukikia.
43018033	Paapo uPilatu nũingĩla mwijumba lya kĩtemi kangĩ, numuĩta ũYesu, numuĩĩla, “Ue uue mutemi wa Ayahũdine?”
